      <script type="text/javascript">
       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_312062").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/312062?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_312062").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_312062").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_312062").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}
      </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var themeActionsBanner = null;
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		themeActionsBanner = jQuery("#theme-actions-banner");
		jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
			if(parseInt(jQuery(this).scrollTop(), 10) &gt; 51) {
				themeActionsBanner.addClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "41px");
			} else {
				themeActionsBanner.removeClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "10px");
			}
		});
	});
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    var logoContainer;
		var infosContainer;
		var logoToHome;
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			logoContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-logo");
			infosContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-infos");

			logoToHome = jQuery("#logoToHome", logoContainer);
			//makes the logo Rumble
			logoToHome.jrumble({
				x: 0,
				y: 0,
				rotation: 4,
				speed: 75
			});
			logoToHome.hover(function() {
				var logo = $(this);
				logo.trigger('startRumble');
				// Stop 500ms after
				setTimeout(function() {
					logo.trigger('stopRumble');
				}, 500);
			}, function(){
				$(this).trigger('stopRumble');
			});
		});
   </script>

								if(thePostToPrintHasBeenClosed){
										return;
				}

					target = jQuery(e.target);

								if (target == null || target.parents(".related-scoops").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents(".feedbackBannerContent").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#headbanner").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#moreInfoBlock").length === 0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#thePostToPrint").length === 0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents(".simplemodal-data").length === 0
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#leadgen-container").length === 0
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-overlay") 
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-data") 
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-close")) {

					thePostToPrintHasBeenClosed = true;

			}

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4044212481">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd%20%20" onclick="trackPostClick(4044212481 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Moodle Course Rental Services
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd%20%20" onclick="trackPostClick(4044212481); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Moodle Course Rental Services | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="278" id="postImage_4044212481" src="http://img.scoop.it/FEO1XAbM8SDWG8-GeI3kSzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 278;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd%20%20" onclick="trackPostClick(4044212481); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .integrating-techn
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   ology
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .org
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/teaching-to-learn-and-learning-to-teach/p/4044212481/2015/05/23/moodle-course-rental-services">
                    May 23, 2:11 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4044212481">
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Dr. Nellie Deutsch's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   As we all know, when it comes to learning skills, practice makes perfect. In the case of Moodling, having a Moodle course of your own is very valuable. I would never have learned how to be a skilled Moodler, had I not had the opportunity to use Moodle in my face-to-face classes and later on fully online. I had no support and invested a great deal of time trying to figure things out. Therefore, I decided to make the process easier for you by providing Moodle course renting services.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Participants of Moodle MOOC 6 can rent out a moodle course area for a year with the option of renewing the space every year. Teachers of the Moodle course can develop a course or install a backup of an existing Moodle course. Course owners will be able to take their courses once they wish to move on to another Moodle area.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Moodle course owners will get full support on how to set up and run their course for the duration of the course. The rental fee is $65. Click here to start the process:
                   <a href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd
                   </a>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Spread the word to other teachers, so they can learn of the opportunity to teach in blended or fully online with full technical and pedagogical support.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                       <span>

                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          As we all know, when it comes to learning skills, practice makes perfect. In the case of Moodling, having a Moodle course of your own is very valuable. I would never have learned how to be a skilled Moodler, had I not had the opportunity to use Moodle in my face-to-face classes and later on fully online. I had no support and invested a great deal of time trying to figure things out. Therefore, I decided to make the process easier for you by providing Moodle course renting services.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Participants of Moodle MOOC 6 can rent out a moodle course area for a year with the option of renewing the space every year. Teachers of the Moodle course can develop a course or install a backup of an existing Moodle course. Course owners will be able to take their courses once they wish to move on to another Moodle area.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Moodle course owners will get full support on how to set up and run their course for the duration of the course. The rental fee is $65. Click here to start the process:
                          <a href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd" rel="nofollow">
                           http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Spread the word to other teachers, so they can learn of the opportunity to teach in blended or fully online with full technical and pedagogical support.
                         </p>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-comment-container" id="comment_69619839">
                     <div class="post-comment">
                      <a class="preview-profile post-comment-avatar-link" href="/u/nellie-deutsch">
                       <img class="post-comment-avatar" height="32px" src="http://img.scoop.it/rKo5L1ncNy9Afv0aFtJ2t3te7K7FKzbUk9Fz-4VREs0=" width="32px"/>
                      </a>
                      <div class="post-comment-delete">
                      </div>
                      <div class="post-comment-content post-comment-insight ">
                       <a class="post-comment-author preview-profile" href="/u/nellie-deutsch">
                        Dr. Nellie Deutsch
                       </a>
                       <span>
                        's curator insight,
                       </span>
                       <span class="post-comment-date">
                        <a class="post-comment-date" href="/t/going-beyond-the-classroom/p/4044212521/2015/05/23/moodle-course-rental-services">
                         May 23, 2:13 AM
                        </a>
                       </span>
                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          As we all know, when it comes to learning skills, practice makes perfect. In the case of Moodling, having a Moodle course of your own is very valuable. I would never have learned how to be a skilled Moodler, had I not had the opportunity to use Moodle in my face-to-face classes and later on fully online. I had no support and invested a great deal of time trying to figure things out. Therefore, I decided to make the process easier for you by providing Moodle course renting services.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Participants of Moodle MOOC 6 can rent out a moodle course area for a year with the option of renewing the space every year. Teachers of the Moodle course can develop a course or install a backup of an existing Moodle course. Course owners will be able to take their courses once they wish to move on to another Moodle area.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Moodle course owners will get full support on how to set up and run their course for the duration of the course. The rental fee is $65. Click here to start the process:
                          <a href="http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd" rel="nofollow">
                           http://www.integrating-technology.org/course/index.php?categoryid=109&amp;lang=gd
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Spread the word to other teachers, so they can learn of the opportunity to teach in blended or fully online with full technical and pedagogical support.
                         </p>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>

                  <div class="title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title">
                   Day 2 of CO15
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Day 2 of CO15 | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="263" id="postImage_4036788168" src="http://img.scoop.it/zZ4yrb1AtNVw3P-0UqkwHjl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 263;" width="467"/>

                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/teaching-to-learn-and-learning-to-teach/p/4036788168/2015/02/07/day-2-of-co15">
                    February 7, 2:57 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4036788168">
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Dr. Nellie Deutsch's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   You're invited to join us for the second day of CO15 as we partner for learning:
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   1. PoodLL on Moodle:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476712-co15-poodll-on-moodle" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476712-co15-poodll-on-moodle
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   2. Organizational aspects in e-learning: the issue of knowledge management:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476713-co15-organizational-aspects-of-e-learning" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476713-co15-organizational-aspects-of-e-learning
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   3. Connecting Online to Improve Instructional Learning:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476724-co15-connecting-online-to-improve-instructional-learning" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476724-co15-connecting-online-to-improve-instructional-learning
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   4. Books on E-learning: Technology That Tutors:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476735-co15-books-on-elearning-technology-that-tutors" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476735-co15-books-on-elearning-technology-that-tutors
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   5. Collaborative Online Learning:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476747-co15-collaborative-online-learning" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476747-co15-collaborative-online-learning
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   6. Using Student Feedback for Continual Improvement of Your Online Course:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476753-co15-student-feedback-for-continual-improvement-of-online-courses" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476753-co15-student-feedback-for-continual-improvement-of-online-courses
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   7. Understanding Pair Work in Micro Teaching Online:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476773-co15-understanding-pair-work-in-micro-teaching-online" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476773-co15-understanding-pair-work-in-micro-teaching-online
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   8. The End of Online Learning - the Beginning of Mobile Acquiring Language Skills:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2480120-co15-end-of-e-learning-and-into-mobile-acquisition-of-language-skills" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2480120-co15-end-of-e-learning-and-into-mobile-acquisition-of-language-skills
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   9. Learning Based on Location- thewandering:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476808-co15-learning-based-on-location-thewandering" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476808-co15-learning-based-on-location-thewandering
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   10. Setting Up and Running a MOOC on WizIQ: Lessons Learned and in Progress:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476812-co15-setting-up-and-running-a-mooc-on-wiziq" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476812-co15-setting-up-and-running-a-mooc-on-wiziq
                   </a>
                   <br/>
                   11. Dealing with difficult students in the online classroom:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476836-co15-dealing-with-difficult-students-in-the-online-classroom" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2476836-co15-dealing-with-difficult-students-in-the-online-classroom
                   </a>
                  </p>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <div class="title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title">
                   Free Bi-Montly IATEFL YLT SIG Webinars on Teaching and Learning
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Free Bi-Montly IATEFL YLT SIG Webinars on Teaching and Learning | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="327" id="postImage_4028842217" src="http://img.scoop.it/fEaoGnqGK4-OKxs7sT4f9jl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 327;" width="467"/>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/teaching-to-learn-and-learning-to-teach/p/4028842217/2014/09/28/free-bi-montly-iatefl-ylt-sig-webinars-on-teaching-and-learning">

                   </a>
                  </span>

                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Dr. Nellie Deutsch's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   Join today's webinar. It's free along with the ones that follow. Just click to join:
                   <a href="http://iateflyltsig.wiziq.com/online-class/2141496-ylt-webinars-the-timeline-of-an-e-connected-story" rel="nofollow">
                    http://iateflyltsig.wiziq.com/online-class/2141496-ylt-webinars-the-timeline-of-an-e-connected-story
                   </a>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   You're invited to learn with other teachers from around the globe. Join IATEFL YLTSIG free bi-monthly webinars. You'll receive reminders of the live online events and watch the recordings as many times as you wish. You'll have an opportunity to learn by engaging with the presenters, the content material of the webinars, and with other educators from around the globe. Just click on the following link:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/course/75751-webinars-for-iatefl-ylt-sig" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/course/75751-webinars-for-iatefl-ylt-sig
                   </a>
                   to join the webinar area.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                  </p>

                  <div class="title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title">
                   Start Teaching with a TESOL Certificate
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Start Teaching with a TESOL Certificate | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="147" id="postImage_4025591039" src="http://img.scoop.it/Nt4E0uFNaDlyAfDb7mMwyTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 147;" width="467"/>

                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Dr. Nellie Deutsch's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   Get a TESOL certificate and start teaching at school (face-to-face or online).
                  </p>
                  <p>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   I will be giving a fully online TESOL certified course. The certificates will be awarded by a well known accredited university in the USA. The course is going to be an intensive 4 week online course. The certificates will each be signed by the dean of the university and sent to your homes by special delivery. I will be teaching the course. Please email me if you're interested at nelliedeutsch@gmail.com
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>

                   Connecting Online Conference for 2014 (CO14)
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Connecting Online Conference for 2014 (CO14) | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="342" id="postImage_4015096908" src="http://img.scoop.it/MtOz3F_a4qoE5OsZkvVL9Tl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 342;" width="467"/>

                   </p>

                   Obsessed with How Teachers Teach
                  </div>

                </div>

                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Obsessed with How Teachers Teach | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="354" id="postImage_4044191488" src="http://img.scoop.it/1-5Bvp0v-09iAVBdlSA9wDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 354;" width="467"/>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2438558-science-of-learning" onclick="trackPostClick(4035486913 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Science of Learning
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2438558-science-of-learning" onclick="trackPostClick(4035486913); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Science of Learning | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="407" id="postImage_4035486913" src="http://img.scoop.it/Z1Km6zk24fuVvN6yabURmzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 407;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>

                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2438558-science-of-learning" onclick="trackPostClick(4035486913); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                  </span>

                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4035486913">
                   <blockquote>
                    The Science of Learning is part of Teaching with Technology free online course on WizIQ. Learning is a natural part of our lives. But what do we know abou
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Dr. Nellie Deutsch's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   Learning is a natural part of our lives. But what do we know about the process of learning? What mechanisms are involved in learning? Is there a science of learning? If so, what is the science of learning and how can teachers apply it in the face-to-face and online classroom?
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   You're invited to join The Science of Learning class in 20 minutes:
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2438558-science-of-learning" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/2438558-science-of-learning
                   </a>
                   Teaching with Technology on
                   <a href="https://www.wiziq.com/course/92339-teaching-with-technology" rel="nofollow">
                    https://www.wiziq.com/course/92339-teaching-with-technology
                   </a>
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          Learn to teach with technology in face-to-face, blended, fully online, and flipped classes for free. You may even get a certificate of completion if you qualify and reflect on 5 presentations (recordings). It's a great learning opportunity so join us, now for a whole month of online learning. Click on the following link to enroll:
                          <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/course/70332-moodle-mooc-5-teaching-with-technology-and-moodle-training-courses" rel="nofollow">
                           http://www.wiziq.com/course/70332-moodle-mooc-5-teaching-with-technology-and-moodle-training-courses
                          </a>
                         </p>
                        </span>
                       </div>

                            traduction libre :
                           </strong>

                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Moodle MOOC 5 commencera le 1 Octobre, 2014
                         </p>
                         <div>
                          <div>
                           <div>
                            <span style="font-size: 14.0px;">
                             Moodle MOOC 5: enseignement des cours de formation et de technologie Moodle :
                            </span>
                            <span style="font-size: 14.0px;">
                             Apprendre  enseigner en ligne  l'aide des technologies Web-Based
                            </span>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                         <div>
                          <p>
                           <span style="">
                            Le thme de ce MOOC est l'apprentissage collaboratif, la pratique rflexive, la connexion en ligne pour l'enseignement et l'apprentissage.
                           </span>
                           <span style="">
                           </span>
                          </p>
                          <p>
                           <span>
                            Le MOOC mettra l'accent sur la connexion en ligne pour l'apprentissage collaboratif et l'enseignement avec : Moodle, Second Life, Mahara, Google Drive Docs et Google Apps, les appareils mobiles, les classes virtuelles...
                           </span>
                          </p>
                          <p>
                           <span>
                            .
                           </span>
                          </p>
                          <p>
                           <span>
                            Moodle MOOC 5 comprendra des cours pour M
                            <span>
                             oodleurs
                            </span>
                            dbutants et avancs .
                           </span>
                          </p>
                          <p>
                           <span>
                            Les cours seront asynchrone (Moodle) et synchrone (WizIQ) avec des enregistrements sur WizIQ, YouTube, et Vimeo.
                           </span>
                          </p>

                   Second Life MOOC for 2014 on WizIQ
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <div class="thisistherealimage">
                   <img alt="Second Life MOOC for 2014 on WizIQ | Teaching to Learn and Learning to Teach | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="410" id="postImage_4018649153" src="http://img.scoop.it/1vbndZUZF6WfvyPqw24Vajl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 410;" width="467"/>

                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   Join us at the SL MOOC opening ceremony tomorrow at your time (2PM EST Toronto time):
                   <a href="http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/1718342-sl-mooc-opening-ceremony-and-what-s-ahead" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.wiziq.com/online-class/1718342-sl-mooc-opening-ceremony-and-what-s-ahead
                   </a>
                   and get information about SLMOOC14 - how the MOOC will work, about WizIQ and the Second Life activities and the activities in the Moodle for Teachers course (where you will get your certificate for presenting and participation.

(function(d, s, id, debug){
    var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
    if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
    js = d.createElement(s); 
    js.id = id;
    js.async=true;
    js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all" + (debug ? "/debug" : "") + ".js";
    fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
  }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk', /*debug*/ false));


window.twttr.ready(function (twttr) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

window.twttr.ready(function (twttr) {
	twttr.events.bind('tweet', function(event) {
		var url = jQuery(event.target).parent().attr("data-unshortenUrl");
		var location = jQuery(event.target).parent().attr("data-location");
		trackNativeButtonShare('twitter', location, url);
	});
});

jQuery(function() {
	jQuery.getScript("//platform.linkedin.com/in.js?async=true", function() {IN.init()});
});

function linkedinShareSuccess(e) {
	var location = jQuery(".linkedin-share-button[data-href='"+e+"']").attr("data-location");
	var url = e;
	trackNativeButtonShare('linkedin', location, url);
}




window.___gcfg = {
    parsetags: 'explicit'
};

(function() {
    var po = document.createElement('script'); po.type = 'text/javascript'; po.async = true;
    po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(po, s);
})();
  
  
function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}
}


function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);
